	}

if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') != '76f2a3ae04e9aa2bae46bb72a37a0b9498cef6b0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '76f2a3ae04e9aa2bae46bb72a37a0b9498cef6b0') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== 'd2588c51f45ca84714650875953b1de1ddc45957') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png') !== '76f2a3ae04e9aa2bae46bb72a37a0b9498cef6b0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/class_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php') !== 'c761b424043844ec5a2e10a8355a4330cb30ae00') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php') !== '7d3bd3f0e12c06c4f85d56c23fe456ee7ca5e54b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 449\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 449') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
